Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Authentication Api's

APIs to manage the user Authentication.

User Login

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"neque\",
    \"password\": \"iure\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "neque",
    "password": "iure"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
    "message": "Hi User Name, welcome",
    "access_token": "254|33icFsR8uIOF1KsOeaJ114ntrU8adIX7gitwAveK",
    "token_type": "Bearer"
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/login

Body Parameters

email  string  

password  string  

user password.

send otp

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/send/otp/quia" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/send/otp/quia"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/send/otp/{number}

URL Parameters

number  string  

verify otp

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/verify/otp/amet/eos" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/verify/otp/amet/eos"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/verify/otp/{number}/{otp}

URL Parameters

number  string  

otp  string  

Checkin Api's

APIs to manage customer checkin

Customer Checkin

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/customer/ea/checkin" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://172.104.245.14/sokoflowadmin/public/api/customer/ea/checkin"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (404):
